This configuration controls the \\\"\\n84:                                                  + \\\"default batch size in bytes. \\\"\\n85:                                                  + \\\"<p>\\\"\\n86:                                                  + \\\"No attempt will be made to batch records larger than this size. \\\"\\n87:                                                  + \\\"<p>\\\"\\n88:                                                  + \\\"Requests sent to brokers will contain multiple batches, one for each partition with data available to be sent. \\\"\\n89:                                                  + \\\"<p>\\\"\\n90:                                                  + \\\"A small batch size will make batching less common and may reduce throughput (a batch size of zero will disable \\\"\\n91:                                                  + \\\"batching entirely). This controls the \\\"\\n125:                                            + \\\" durability of records that are sent. The following settings are allowed: \\\"\\n126:                                            + \\\" <ul>\\\"\\n127:                                            + \\\" <li><code>acks=0</code> If set to zero then the producer will not wait for any acknowledgment from the\\\"\\n128:                                            + \\\" server at all. However in some circumstances the client may want to \\\"\\n147:                                                 + \\\"reduce the number of requests even under moderate load. CommonClientConfigs.postValidateSaslMechanismConfig(this);\n558:         CommonClientConfigs.warnDisablingExponentialBackoff(this);\n559:         Map<String, Object> refinedConfigs = CommonClientConfigs.postProcessReconnectBackoffConfigs(this, parsedValues);\n560:         postProcessAndValidateIdempotenceConfigs(refinedConfigs);\n561:         maybeOverrideClientId(refinedConfigs);\n562:         return refinedConfigs;\n563:     }\n564: \n565:     private void maybeOverrideClientId(final Map<String, Object> configs) {\n566:         String refinedClientId;\n567:         boolean userConfiguredClientId = this.originals().containsKey(CLIENT_ID_CONFIG);\n568:         if (userConfiguredClientId) {\n569:             refinedClientId = this.getString(CLIENT_ID_CONFIG);\n570:         } else {\n571:             String transactionalId = this.getString(TRANSACTIONAL_ID_CONFIG);\n572:             refinedClientId = \"producer-\" + (transactionalId != null ? transactionalId : PRODUCER_CLIENT_ID_SEQUENCE.getAndIncrement());\n573:         }\n574:         configs.put(CLIENT_ID_CONFIG, refinedClientId);\n575:     }\n576: \n577:     private void postProcessAndValidateIdempotenceConfigs(final Map<String, Object> configs) {\n578:         final Map<String, Object> originalConfigs = this.originals();\n579:         final String acksStr = parseAcks(this.getString(ACKS_CONFIG));\n580:         configs.put(ACKS_CONFIG, acksStr);\n581:         final boolean userConfiguredIdempotence = this.originals().containsKey(ENABLE_IDEMPOTENCE_CONFIG);\n582:         boolean idempotenceEnabled = this.getBoolean(ENABLE_IDEMPOTENCE_CONFIG);\n583:         boolean shouldDisableIdempotence = false;\n584: \n585:         // For idempotence producers, values for `retries` and `acks` and `max.in.flight.requests.per.connection` need validation\n586:         if (idempotenceEnabled) {\n587:             final int retries = this.getInt(RETRIES_CONFIG);\n588:             if (retries == 0) {\n589:                 if (userConfiguredIdempotence) {\n590:                     throw new ConfigException(\"Must set \" + RETRIES_CONFIG + \" to non-zero when using the idempotent producer.\");\n591:                 }\n592:                 log.info(\"Idempotence will be disabled because {} is set to 0.\", RETRIES_CONFIG);\n593:                 shouldDisableIdempotence = true;\n594:             }\n595: \n596:             final short acks = Short.parseShort(acksStr);\n597:             if (acks != (short) -1) {\n598:                 if (userConfiguredIdempotence) {\n599:                     throw new ConfigException(\"Must set \" + ACKS_CONFIG + \" to all in order to use the idempotent Sender Storage (Producer Side)**\\nThe `Sender` class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java) stores the `acks` value as a private field (line 99) and receives it via the constructor (line 134). This field represents the number of acknowledgments the producer requires the leader to have received before considering a request complete.\\n\\n**4. Protocol Encoding (Producer Client - Network)**\\nThe `acks` value is encoded into the produce request protocol at line 899 in `Sender.java` via `new ProduceRequestData().setAcks(acks)`. The protocol specification is defined in `ProduceRequest.json` (line 55-56) which specifies `Acks` as an `int16` field representing the number of acknowledgments (0 for no acknowledgments, 1 for only the leader, -1 for the full in-sync replica set (ISR)).\\n\\n**5.
